CRI consists of a protocol buffers and gRPC API.\\n15: Read more about CRI at [kubernetes docs](https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/architecture/cri/).\\n16: \\n17: The repository [kubernetes/cri-client](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-client) is a mirror of https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/tree/master/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client.\\n18: Please do **not** file issues or submit PRs against the [kubernetes/cri-client](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-client)\\n19: repository as it is readonly, all development is done in [kubernetes/kubernetes](https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes).\\n20: \",\"endLine\":20,\"startLine\":11},{\"content\":\"5: \\n6: # cri-client\\n7: \\n8: Container Runtime Interface client implementation\\n9: \\n10: \",\"endLine\":10,\"startLine\":5},{\"content\":\"20: \\n21: The [`cri-api` staging repository](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-api) is\\n22: defined in [kubernetes/kubernetes](https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes)\\n23: and is **only** intended to be used for kubelet to container runtime\\n24: interactions, or for node-level troubleshooting using a tool such as `crictl`.\\n25: The `cri-api` wraps the [Protobuf protocol definition](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-api/blob/63929b3/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto)\\n26: with extra features which can be used directly from other clients as well.\\n27: It is **not** a common purpose container runtime API for general use, and is\\n28: intended to be Kubernetes-centric. CRI consists of a protocol buffers and gRPC API.\n15: Read more about CRI at [kubernetes docs](https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/architecture/cri/).\n16: \n17: The repository [kubernetes/cri-client](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-client) is a mirror of https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/tree/master/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client.\n18: Please do **not** file issues or submit PRs against the [kubernetes/cri-client](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-client)\n19: repository as it is readonly, all development is done in [kubernetes/kubernetes](https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes).\n20: ","endLine":20,"startLine":11},{"content":"5: \n6: # cri-client\n7: \n8: Container Runtime Interface client implementation\n9: \n10: ","endLine":10,"startLine":5},{"content":"20: \n21: The [`cri-api` staging repository](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-api) is\n22: defined in [kubernetes/kubernetes](https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes)\n23: and is **only** intended to be used for kubelet to container runtime\n24: interactions, or for node-level troubleshooting using a tool such as `crictl`.\n25: The `cri-api` wraps the [Protobuf protocol definition](https://github.com/kubernetes/cri-api/blob/63929b3/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto)\n26: with extra features which can be used directly from other clients as well.\n27: It is **not** a common purpose container runtime API for general use, and is\n28: intended to be Kubernetes-centric. We try to avoid it, but there may be logic\n29: within a container runtime that optimizes for the order or specific parameters\n30: of call(s) that the kubelet makes.\n31: ","endLine":31,"startLine":20}],"file":"staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/README.md","repo":"github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes","type":"file","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/README.md"},{"chunks":[{"content":"878: func (ipc ImagePullCheck) Check() (warnings, errorList []error) {\n879: \tcontainerRuntime := utilruntime.NewContainerRuntime(ipc.criSocket)\n880: \tif ipc.impl != nil {\n881: \t\tcontainerRuntime.SetImpl(ipc.impl)\n882: \t}\n883: \tif err := containerRuntime.Connect(); If such an\\n45: // incident happens, GenenricPLEG would miss all events regarding this\\n46: // container. In the case of relisting failure, the window may become longer.\\n47: // Note that this assumption is not unique -- many kubelet internal components\\n48: // rely on terminated containers as tombstones for bookkeeping purposes. The\\n49: // garbage collector is implemented to work with such situations.
